Layering and absolute postioning

Layered Pane

The layered pane arranges PANE components in a vertical order. The first PANE below the component is drawn in the back, the next on top of the previous one.

All the PANEs cover the whole available area that is given by LAYEREDPANE. If no size is defined with LAYEREDPANE then the biggest contained PANE defines the size of the whole LAYEREDPANE.

PAY ATTENTION: the top pane (which is the last PANE in the sequence below LAYEREDPANE) is catching all the mouse events - so it does not make sense to arrange any input components within a background pane.

Typical usage: you display some information "in the back" and want to have some active components on top of it.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoLayeredPane}" >
  <t:row id="g_2" >
    <t:layeredpane id="g_3" bgpaint="rectangle(0,0,100%,100%,#80808030)" height="200" width="200" >
      <t:pane id="g_4" >
        <t:row id="g_5" >
          <t:image id="g_6" height="100" image="#{d.DemoLayeredPane.p.image}" width="100" />
          <t:coldistance id="g_7" width="5" />
          <t:label id="g_8" font="size:20" text="#{d.DemoLayeredPane.p.name}" />
        </t:row>
        <t:row id="g_9" >
          <t:textpane id="g_10" text="#{d.DemoLayeredPane.p.comment}" width="100%" />
        </t:row>
      </t:pane>
      <t:pane id="g_11" bgpaint="rectangle(0,0,60,100%,#FFFFFF80)" >
        <t:rowdistance id="g_12" height="100%" />
        <t:row id="g_13" >
          <t:button id="g_14" actionListener="#{d.DemoLayeredPane.onNext}" text="Next" width="60" />
        </t:row>
      </t:pane>
    </t:layeredpane>
  </t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoLayeredPane}")

public class DemoLayeredPane 
    extends PageBean
    implements Serializable
{
    static Planet[] PLANET = new Planet[] 
    {
        new Planet("Mercury","This is a comment about Mercury. This is a comment about Mercury.","/images/pictures/photo0.gif"),
        new Planet("Venus","This is a comment about Venus. This is a comment about Venus.","/images/pictures/photo1.gif"),
        new Planet("Earth","This is a comment about the Earth. This is a comment about the Earth. This is a comment about the Earth.","/images/pictures/photo2.gif"),
    };
    
    public static class Planet implements java.io.Serializable
    {
        public Planet(String name, String comment, String image)
        {
            super();
            m_name = name;
            m_comment = comment;
            m_image = image;
        }

        protected String m_image;
        public String getImage() { return m_image; }
        public void setImage(String value) { m_image = value; }

        protected String m_comment;
        public String getComment() { return m_comment; }
        public void setComment(String value) { m_comment = value; }

        protected String m_name;
        public String getName() { return m_name; }
        public void setName(String value) { m_name = value; }
    }

    int m_selectedIndex = 0;
    
    public DemoLayeredPane(IWorkpageDispatcher dispatcher)
    {
        super(dispatcher);
    }

    public Planet getP() { return PLANET[m_selectedIndex]; }
    
    public void onNext(ActionEvent ae)
    {
        m_selectedIndex++;
        if (m_selectedIndex >= PLANET.length)
            m_selectedIndex = 0;
    }
}

Layered Pane with PAINTAREA

This demo shows a typical use case for the LAYEREDPANE component:

In the background layer some image is positioned.

In the foreground layer some buttons are arrangd using the PAINTAREA component, that allows to absolutely define the position of a component.

This is the XML layout definition:

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.defaultscreens.OKPopup;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.BaseActionEvent;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDispatchedPageBean;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoLayeredPanePaintArea}")

public class DemoLayeredPanePaintArea
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoLayeredPanePaintArea(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demolayeredpanepaintarea.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoLayeredPanePaintArea}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public void onButtonAction(ActionEvent event) 
    {
        BaseActionEvent e = (BaseActionEvent)event;
        String ref = e.getSourceReference();
        OKPopup.createInstance("Button pressed","The reference behind the button is: " + ref);
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Overlaying of components

The OVERLAYAREA is a container holding OVERLAYAREAAREAITEM components which themselves are containers to hold any other component.

The OVERLAYAREA components are positioned by assigning an explicit x-y-width-height-z definition. Width and height are optional - if not explicitly defined then the component is sized by its minimum size.

This demo shows the usage of the property BOUNDSANCHOR that defined to which point of the item the x,y-position is applied.

This is the XML layout definition:

Status message area on top of grid

The PAINTAREA is some generic contain that manages content within PAINTAREAITEM elements.

In the example some message area is drawn on top of the grid.

Each PAINTAREAITEM content is absolutely positioned. Positions are passed via the BOUNDS property either in pixels ("100") or as percentage figure ("30%"). In addition there is a BOUNDSANCHOR attribute that is used to define the point of the item to which the x/y position is applied.

Optional part of the BOUNDS definition is a z-index ("x;y;width;height;z-index"). Components with higher z-index are drawn on top of components with lower z-index.

Please make sure that you set attribute MOVETOFRONTONMOUSEOVER to "false" - at least for the components that you want to always be kept in the background (in the example: the PAINTAREAITEM containing the grid).

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage}" rowdistance="10" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:coldistance id="g_3" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_4" actionListener="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.onHideShowAction}" text="Hide / Show message area" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_5" >
<t:overlayarea id="g_6" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:overlayareabaseitem id="g_7" >
<t:fixgrid id="g_8" height="100%" objectbinding="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.grid}" sbvisibleamount="35" width="100%" >
<t:gridcol id="g_9" text="First Name" width="50%" >
<t:label id="g_10" text=".{firstName}" />
</t:gridcol>
<t:gridcol id="g_11" text="Last Name" width="50%" >
<t:label id="g_12" text=".{lastName}" />
</t:gridcol>
</t:fixgrid>
</t:overlayareabaseitem>
<t:overlayareaitem id="g_13" background="#FFC0C0C0" border="left:1;right:1;top:1;bottom:0;color:#00000030" boundsanchor="centerbottom" height="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.messaageAraeHeight}" width="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.messageAreaWidth}" x="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.messageAreaX}" y="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.messageAreaY}" zindex="2" >
<t:pane id="g_14" padding="left:10;right:10;top:0;bottom:0" >
<t:row id="g_15" >
<t:awesomefonticon id="g_16" contentareafilled="false" foreground="#800000" iconhexcode="f25a" iconsize="30" />
<t:label id="g_17" align="center" font="weight:bold" height="100%" text="Too many items found! Please restrict your selection." width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:overlayareaitem>
</t:overlayarea>
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_18" coldistance="5" >
<t:coldistance id="g_19" width="50%" />
<t:label id="g_29" align="center" text="x/y/width/height:" />
<t:label id="g_20" text="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.messageAreaX}" />
<t:label id="g_31" text="/" />
<t:label id="g_21" text="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.messageAreaY}" />
<t:label id="g_33" text="/" />
<t:label id="g_22" text="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.messageAreaWidth}" />
<t:label id="g_34" text="/" />
<t:label id="g_23" text="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage.messaageAraeHeight}" />
<t:coldistance id="g_24" width="50%" />
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.impl.FIXGRIDItem;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.impl.FIXGRIDListBinding;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.util.Trigger;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDispatchedPageBean;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage}")

public class DemoPaintAreaUsage
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public class GridItem extends FIXGRIDItem implements java.io.Serializable
    {
        String m_lastName;
        public String getLastName() { return m_lastName; }
        public void setLastName(String value) { this.m_lastName = value; }

        String m_firstName;
        public String getFirstName() { return m_firstName; }
        public void setFirstName(String value) { this.m_firstName = value; }
    }


    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    private boolean m_messageAreaShown = true;
    String m_messageAreaX = "50%";
    String m_messageAreaY = "100%";
    String m_messageAreaWidth = "400";
    String m_messaageAraeHeight = "100";
    FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem> m_grid = new FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem>();

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoPaintAreaUsage(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
        for (int i=0; i<100; i++)
        {
            GridItem gi = new GridItem();
            gi.setFirstName("First " + (i+1));
            gi.setLastName("Last " + (i+1));
            m_grid.getItems().add(gi);
        }
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demopaintareausage.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoPaintAreaUsage}"; }

    public String getMessageAreaX() { return m_messageAreaX; }
    public String getMessageAreaY() { return m_messageAreaY; }
    public String getMessageAreaWidth() { return m_messageAreaWidth; }
    public String getMessaageAraeHeight() { return m_messaageAraeHeight; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem> getGrid() { return m_grid; }

    public void onHideShowAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_messageAreaShown = !m_messageAreaShown;
        if (m_messageAreaShown == true)
        {
            m_messageAreaWidth = "400";
            m_messaageAraeHeight = "100";
        }
        else
        {
            m_messageAreaWidth = "100";
            m_messaageAraeHeight = "0";
        }
    }
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Show content on mouse over only

Certain content is only shown if the user moves with the mouse in top of the component.

The component to be used is the OVERLAYAREA - internally showing OVERLAYAREAITEMS. For each item you can set a flag SHOWONAREAMOUSEOVERONLY to "true" - as consequence this item will only be shown, if the user moves the mouse on top of the area on top.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>

Fields on top of form

This demo shows absolutely positioned FIELDs on top of some real form.

The demo includes some editor: you can create new FIELD instances by using the right-mouse-button popup-menu and you can move and resize the FIELD instances.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoFormInput}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_2" objectbinding="#{d.DemoFormInput}" rowdistance="0" >
<t:rowheader id="g_3" >
<t:button id="g_4" actionListener="#{d.DemoFormInput.onSaveAction}" text="Save" width="100+" />
<t:coldistance id="g_5" width="50%" />
<t:slider id="g_6" flush="true" majortickspacing="25" maxvalue="200" minortickspacing="5" minvalue="50" value="#{d.DemoFormInput.scaleInt}" width="300" />
<t:coldistance id="g_7" width="50%" />
</t:rowheader>
<t:row id="g_8" >
<t:scrollpane id="g_9" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_10" >
<t:scalepane id="g_11" height="100%" scale="#{d.DemoFormInput.scale}" width="100%" >
<t:paintarea id="g_12" actionListener="#{d.DemoFormInput.onCreateNewFieldAction}" background="#FFFFFF" height="100%" popupmenu="PAINTAREA" width="100%" >
<t:paintareaitem id="g_13" bounds="0;0;1000;1426;1" boundsanchor="lefttop" >
<t:image id="g_14" height="1426" image="/images/pictures/kfzbrief.jpg" width="1000" />
</t:paintareaitem>
<t:repeat id="g_15" listbinding="#{d.DemoFormInput.fields}" >
<t:paintareaitem id="g_16" actionListener=".{onItemAction}" bounds=".{bounds}" movingenabled="true" popupmenu="FIELDITEM" resizingenabled="true" >
<t:pane id="g_17" cutheight="true" cutwidth="true" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_18" >
<t:field id="g_19" background="#FFFFFF" height="100%" text=".{value}" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:paintareaitem>
</t:repeat>
</t:paintarea>
</t:scalepane>
</t:row>
</t:scrollpane>
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:popupmenu id="PAINTAREA" >
<t:menuitem id="g_20" command="CREATENEWFIELD" text="Create new field" />
</t:popupmenu>
<t:popupmenu id="FIELDITEM" >
<t:menuitem id="g_21" command="REMOVEFIELD" text="Remove field" />
</t:popupmenu>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.events.BaseActionEventPopupMenuItem;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.streamstore.StreamStore;
import org.eclnt.util.file.ClassloaderReader;
import org.eclnt.util.log.CLog;
import org.eclnt.util.valuemgmt.ValueManager;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoFormInput}")
public class DemoFormInput
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public class FieldsItem extends Object implements java.io.Serializable
    {
        String i_value;
        int i_height;
        int i_width;
        int i_y;
        int i_x;
        public String getValue() { return i_value; }
        public void setValue(String value) { this.i_value = value; }
        public int getHeight() { return i_height; }
        public int getWidth() { return i_width; }
        public int getY() { return i_y; }
        public int getX() { return i_x; }
        public String getBounds() { return i_x+";"+i_y+";"+i_width+";"+i_height+";2"; }
        public void setBounds(String value)
        {
            String[] values = ValueManager.decodeCSV(value);
            setBounds(values);
        }
        private void setBounds(String[] values)
        {
            i_x = ValueManager.decodeInt(values[0],0);
            i_y = ValueManager.decodeInt(values[1],0);
            i_width = ValueManager.decodeInt(values[2],100);
            i_height = ValueManager.decodeInt(values[3],20);
        }
        public void onItemAction(ActionEvent event)
        {
            if (event instanceof BaseActionEventPopupMenuItem)
            {
                BaseActionEventPopupMenuItem e = (BaseActionEventPopupMenuItem)event;
                if  ("REMOVEFIELD".equals(e.getCommand()))
                {
                    m_fields.remove(this);
                }
            }
        }
        private String toCSV()
        {
            return ValueManager.encodeCSV(new String[] {""+i_x,""+i_y,""+i_width,""+i_height,i_value});
        }
    }
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    List<FieldsItem> m_fields = new ArrayList<FieldsItem>();
    int m_scaleInt = 100;

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoFormInput(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
        readFields();
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoforminput.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoFormInput}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public List<FieldsItem> getFields() { return m_fields; }
    public int getScaleInt() { return m_scaleInt; }
    public void setScaleInt(int value) { this.m_scaleInt = value; }
    public float getScale() { return ((float)m_scaleInt)/100f; }

    public void onCreateNewFieldAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (event instanceof BaseActionEventPopupMenuItem)
        {
            BaseActionEventPopupMenuItem e = (BaseActionEventPopupMenuItem)event;
            FieldsItem fi = new FieldsItem();
            fi.i_x = e.getPixelX();
            fi.i_y = e.getPixelY();
            fi.i_width = 100;
            fi.i_height = 25;
            m_fields.add(fi);
        }
    }

    public void onSaveAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        saveFields();
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    private void saveFields()
    {
        StringBuffer all = new StringBuffer();
        for (FieldsItem fi: m_fields)
            all.append(fi.toCSV()+"\n");
        StreamStore.getInstance().writeUTF8("/ccdemos/DemoFormInput.csv",all.toString(),true);
    }
    
    private void readFields()
    {
        String txt = StreamStore.getInstance().readUTF8("/ccdemos/DemoFormInput.csv",false);
        if (txt == null)
        {
            txt = new ClassloaderReader(true).readUTF8File("/workplace/DemoFormInput.csv",true);
            txt = txt.replace("\r","");
        }
        String[] csvLines = ValueManager.tokenize(txt,"\n");
        for (String csv: csvLines)
        {
            try
            {
                FieldsItem fi = new FieldsItem();
                String[] values = ValueManager.decodeCSV(csv);
                fi.setBounds(values);
                fi.i_value = values[4];
                m_fields.add(fi);
            }
            catch (Throwable t)
            {
                CLog.L.log(CLog.LL_INF,"Could not parse csv: " + csv);
            }
        }
    }
}

Blur / frozen glass styling

This examples shows how to nicely use the "backdrop-filter" styling of HTML/CSS. It is included in the PANE-stylevariant "ccblur" and is also available as style variant for ROWBODYPANE and as style sequence "riscdialog_popup_blur" for popups.

Of course you can add own style classes and style variants to take use of this feature as well.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>

Positioning in free style HTML

Controls embedded in HTML text

The component TEXTWITHCONTROLS allows to add any component into a free style HTML text.

In the text you need to reference the component by a placeholder with the format "@@<componentId>@@". The component has to be listed as sub-component accordingly.

Please pay attention: if you explicitly size your components, then do not use percentage width and percentage height definitions. They are not supported in the context of TEXTWITHCONTROLS.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoTextWithControls}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_4" objectbinding="#{d.DemoTextWithControls}" >
<t:row id="g_6" >
<t:textwithcontrols id="g_2" height="100%" popupmenu="TEXT" text="&lt;h1&gt;Hello World!&lt;/h1&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Step 1&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Please first input your &lt;b&gt;first name&lt;/b&gt; @@firstname@@ then input your &lt;b&gt;last name&lt;/b&gt; @@lastname@@.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Step 2&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Then press this button: @@hello@@.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Step 3&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;The result then is output into this label: @@result@@.&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;If you want to clear the content of the fields: press this button @@clear@@.&lt;/p&gt;" width="100%" >
<t:field id="firstname" labeltext="First name" text="#{d.DemoTextWithControls.firstName}" width="150" />
<t:field id="lastname" labeltext="Last name" text="#{d.DemoTextWithControls.lastName}" width="150" />
<t:button id="hello" actionListener="#{d.DemoTextWithControls.onHelloAction}" image="/images/iconssvg/ztest_16x16.svg" text="Say Hello" />
<t:label id="result" background="#00000030" labeltext="Result" text="#{d.DemoTextWithControls.result}" />
<t:button id="clear" actionListener="#{d.DemoTextWithControls.onClearAction}" text="Clear fields" />
</t:textwithcontrols>
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:popupmenu id="TEXT" >
<t:menuitem id="g_11" actionListener="#{d.DemoTextWithControls.onClearAction}" text="Clear fields" />
</t:popupmenu>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoTextWithControls}")

public class DemoTextWithControls
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    String m_lastName;
    String m_firstName;
    String m_result = "not yet defined";

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoTextWithControls(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demotextwithcontrols.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoTextWithControls}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public void onClearAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_firstName = null;
        m_lastName = null;
        m_result = "not yet defined";
    }

    public void onHelloAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_result = "Hello world, " + m_firstName + " " + m_lastName + "!";
    }

    public String getResult() { return m_result; }
    public void setResult(String value) { this.m_result = value; }

    public String getLastName() { return m_lastName; }
    public void setLastName(String value) { this.m_lastName = value; }

    public String getFirstName() { return m_firstName; }
    public void setFirstName(String value) { this.m_firstName = value; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Embedding into normal forms

The TEXTWITHCONTROLS component can be embedded into normal form processing. If you only the defined the width of the component then the height will be calculated corresponding to the content.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoTextWithControls2}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_4" objectbinding="#{d.DemoTextWithControls2}" rowdistance="20" >
<t:row id="g_6" >
<t:foldablepane id="g_7" text="Some first container" width="100%" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_9" >
<t:foldablepane id="g_10" text="Some second container with free style text" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:textwithcontrols id="g_3" text="Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consetetur sadipscing elitr. Please define the first name @@fn@@ and the last name @@ln@@. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consetetur sadipscing elitr, sed diam nonumy eirmod tempor invidunt ut labore et dolore magna aliquyam erat, sed diam voluptua.&lt;br&gt;Clear the content of this area by pressing the button @@cl@@.&lt;br&gt;Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consetetur sadipscing elitr, sed diam nonumy eirmod tempor invidunt ut labore et dolore magna aliquyam erat, sed diam voluptua." width="100%" >
<t:field id="fn" text="#{d.DemoTextWithControls2.firstName}" width="100" />
<t:field id="ln" text="#{d.DemoTextWithControls2.lastName}" width="100" />
<t:button id="cl" actionListener="#{d.DemoTextWithControls2.onClearAction}" text="Clear" width="100+" />
</t:textwithcontrols>
</t:row>
</t:foldablepane>
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_18" >
<t:foldablepane id="g_13" text="Some third container" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_15" >
<t:calendarfield id="g_16" labeltext="Delivery date" timezone="LOCAL" value="#{d.DemoTextWithControls2.deliveryDate}" width="200" />
</t:row>
</t:foldablepane>
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.time.LocalDate;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDispatchedPageBean;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoTextWithControls2}")

public class DemoTextWithControls2
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    LocalDate m_deliveryDate = LocalDate.now();
    String m_firstName = "Captain";
    String m_lastName = "Casa";

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoTextWithControls2(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demotextwithcontrols2.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoTextWithControls2}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public void onClearAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_lastName = "";
        m_firstName = "";
    }

    public LocalDate getDeliveryDate() { return m_deliveryDate; }
    public void setDeliveryDate(LocalDate value) { this.m_deliveryDate = value; }

    public String getLastName() { return m_lastName; }
    public void setLastName(String value) { this.m_lastName = value; }

    public String getFirstName() { return m_firstName; }
    public void setFirstName(String value) { this.m_firstName = value; }

}

Example: order letter

This example shows the usage of TEXTWITHCONTROLS in order to define some kind of "order letter".

The text is read from a server side template file. The template file is updated on server side first (title and last name are added to the text).

Please observe on of the disadvantages: when updating the text on server side (e.g. by changing the last name), then the whole template is reprocessed: the focus gets lost and you see a fast flickering.

Use the TEXTWITHCONTROLS if you really want to provide some templating as part of your application or if you want to provide some layout to the user which is close to some print layout.

Do not use it for "normal layouting" of your components!

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoOrderLetter}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_4" objectbinding="#{d.DemoOrderLetter}" >
<t:row id="g_7" >
<t:scrollpane id="g_8" border="#00000010" height="100%" padding="10" shadow="hoffset:4;voffset:4;blur:4;color:#00000020" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_6" >
<t:textwithcontrols id="g_36" text="#{d.DemoOrderLetter.text}" width="100%" >
<t:combobox id="title" flush="true" placeholder="Title" value="#{d.DemoOrderLetter.title}" width="80" >
<t:comboboxitem id="g_5" text="Mr." value="Mr." />
<t:comboboxitem id="g_37" text="Mrs" value="Mrs" />
</t:combobox>
<t:field id="firstName" flush="true" placeholder="First name" text="#{d.DemoOrderLetter.firstName}" width="150" />
<t:field id="lastName" flush="true" placeholder="Last Name" text="#{d.DemoOrderLetter.lastName}" width="150" />
<t:field id="city" flush="true" placeholder="City" text="#{d.DemoOrderLetter.city}" width="150" />
<t:field id="zipCode" flush="true" placeholder="Zip code" text="#{d.DemoOrderLetter.zipCode}" width="80" />
<t:combobox id="country" flush="true" placeholder="Country" value="#{d.DemoOrderLetter.country}" width="150" >
<t:comboboxitem id="g_11" text="Germany" value="DE" />
<t:comboboxitem id="g_12" text="United States" value="US" />
</t:combobox>
<t:pane id="order" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue[&#39;@defaultrowdistance@&#39;]}" width="600" >
<t:row id="g_16" >

<t:button id="g_19" actionListener="#{d.DemoOrderLetter.onNewItemAction}" text="New item" width="100+" />
</t:row>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.time.LocalDate;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.impl.FIXGRIDItem;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.impl.FIXGRIDListBinding;
import org.eclnt.util.file.ClassloaderReader;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDispatchedPageBean;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoOrderLetter}")

public class DemoOrderLetter
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public class GridItem extends FIXGRIDItem implements java.io.Serializable
    {
        BigDecimal i_price;
        public BigDecimal getPrice() { return i_price; }
        public void setPrice(BigDecimal value) { this.i_price = value; }

        int i_quantity;
        public int getQuantity() { return i_quantity; }
        public void setQuantity(int value) { this.i_quantity = value; }

        String i_article;
        public String getArticle() { return i_article; }
        public void setArticle(String value) { this.i_article = value; }

        public void onRemoveAction(ActionEvent event)
        {
            m_grid.getItems().remove(this);
        }
        
        public void onRowSelect()
        {
        }
        public void onRowExecute()
        {
        }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    LocalDate m_paymentDate;
    String m_template;
    String m_text;
    String m_country;
    String m_city;
    String m_street;
    String m_zipCode;
    String m_firstName;
    String m_lastName;
    String m_title;
    FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem> m_grid = new FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem>();
    BigDecimal m_total;
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoOrderLetter(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
        m_template = new ClassloaderReader(true).readUTF8File("/workplace/DemoOrderLetter.html",true);
        updateText();
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoorderletter.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoOrderLetter}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public String getText() { return m_text; } 
    
    public String getCountry() { return m_country; }
    public void setCountry(String value) { this.m_country = value; }

    public String getCity() { return m_city; }
    public void setCity(String value) { this.m_city = value; }

    public String getStreet() { return m_street; }
    public void setStreet(String value) { this.m_street = value; }

    public String getZipCode() { return m_zipCode; }
    public void setZipCode(String value) { this.m_zipCode = value; }

    public String getLastName() { return m_lastName; }
    public void setLastName(String value) { this.m_lastName = value; updateText(); }

    public String getFirstName() { return m_firstName; }
    public void setFirstName(String value) { this.m_firstName = value; }

    public String getTitle() { return m_title; }
    public void setTitle(String value) { this.m_title = value; updateText(); }

    public LocalDate getPaymentDate() { return m_paymentDate; }
    public void setPaymentDate(LocalDate value) { this.m_paymentDate = value; }

    public BigDecimal getTotal()
    {
        m_total = new BigDecimal(0);
        for (GridItem gi: m_grid.getItems())
        {
            m_total = m_total.add(gi.getPrice());
        }
        return m_total;
    }

    public FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem> getGrid() { return m_grid; }
    
    public void onNewItemAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        GridItem gi = new GridItem();
        gi.setArticle("...please define article...");
        gi.setQuantity(1);
        gi.setPrice(new BigDecimal("10.99"));
        m_grid.getItems().add(gi);
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    private void updateText()
    {
        // the template text contains placeholders which are resolved within the
        // text (title and last name)
        m_text = m_template;
        String title = getTitle();
        if (title == null) title = "(title unknown)";
        m_text = m_text.replace("||title||",title);
        String lastName = getLastName();
        if (lastName == null) lastName = "(last name unknown)";
        m_text = m_text.replace("||lastName||",lastName);
    }
}

<br>

<br>
we hereby confirm to deliver the following items:<br>
<br>
@@order@@<br>
<br>

<br>

<br>
Andrew Stevenson<br>
SVP Company XZY
 
*/

Outside-in sizing "Excel"

This HTML was created by some Excel export. The controls placed inside are multiline TEXTEDITOR components.

Please observe: the table resizes the height of the components on input.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_4" objectbinding="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel}" >
<t:row id="g_10" >
<t:combobox id="g_13" actionListener="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel.onHtmlTemplateAction}" flush="true" labeltext="HTML template" validvaluesbinding="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel.htmlTemplateVVS}" value="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel.htmlTemplate}" width="300" />
<t:coldistance id="g_2" width="50" />
<t:button id="g_15" actionListener="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel.onReloadAction}" hotkey="alt-82" text="Reload HTML" width="100+" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_6" >
<t:textwithcontrolsois id="g_8" avoidsanitizing="true" text="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel.htmlText}" width="100%" >
<t:dynamiccontent id="g_11" contentbinding="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel.dynContent}" />
</t:textwithcontrolsois>
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.componentnodes.TEXTEDITORNode;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.impl.DYNAMICCONTENTBinding;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.impl.ROWDYNAMICCONTENTBinding.ComponentNode;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.util.ValidValuesBinding;
import org.eclnt.util.file.ClassloaderReader;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel}")

public class DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    ValidValuesBinding m_htmlTemplateVVS = new ValidValuesBinding();
    String m_htmlTemplate = "oissampleexcel1.html";
    String m_htmlText;
    DYNAMICCONTENTBinding m_dynContent = new DYNAMICCONTENTBinding();
    Map<String,String> m_data = new HashMap<String,String>();
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);
        m_htmlTemplateVVS.addValidValue("oissampleexcel1.html","oissampleexcel1.html");
        m_htmlTemplateVVS.addValidValue("oissampleexcel2.html","oissampleexcel2.html");
        m_htmlTemplateVVS.addValidValue("oissampleexcel3.html","oissampleexcel3.html");
        readHTMLText();
        createFields();
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demotextwithcontrolsoisexcel.xml"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoTextWithControlsOISExcel}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public ValidValuesBinding getHtmlTemplateVVS() { return m_htmlTemplateVVS; }
    public String getHtmlTemplate() { return m_htmlTemplate; }
    public void setHtmlTemplate(String value) { this.m_htmlTemplate = value; }
    public String getHtmlText() { return m_htmlText; }
    public Map<String, String> getData() { return m_data; } 
    public DYNAMICCONTENTBinding getDynContent() { return m_dynContent; }

    public void onReloadAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_htmlText = m_htmlText + " ";
    }

    public void onHtmlTemplateAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event)
    {
        readHTMLText();
        createFields();
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    private void readHTMLText()
    {
        m_htmlText = new ClassloaderReader(true).readUTF8File("/workplace/resources/"+m_htmlTemplate,true);
    }

    private void createFields()
    {
        m_data.clear();
        int counter = 0;
        List<String> ids = findIds();
        List<ComponentNode> l = new ArrayList<ComponentNode>();
        for (String id: ids)
        {
            TEXTEDITORNode f = new TEXTEDITORNode()
//            FIELDNode f = new FIELDNode()
                .setId(id)
                .setText(pbx("data."+id))
                .setAlign("left");
            l.add(f);
            m_data.put(id,"Value " + counter);
            counter++;
        }
        m_dynContent.setContentNodes(l);
    }
    
    private List<String> findIds()
    {
        List<String> result = new ArrayList<String>();
        int currentIndex = 0;
        while (true)
        {
            int pos1 = m_htmlText.indexOf("@@",currentIndex);
            if (pos1 < 0) break;
            int pos2 = m_htmlText.indexOf("@@",pos1+2);
            if (pos2 < 0) break;
            result.add(m_htmlText.substring(pos1+2,pos2));
            currentIndex = pos2+2;
        }
        return result;
    }
    
}

Adaptive Containers - Controls

Flexible lines

The special row component ROWFLEXLINECONTAINER holds components which are distributed to one or more optical rows - according to the size of the components.

Only use absolute sizes for sizing the contained components - not percentage values.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoRowFlexLineContainer}" rowdistance="10" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_3" text="Resize the screen horizontally - the images below will be re-arranged accordingly." />
</t:row>
<t:rowflexlinecontainer id="g_4" align="#{d.DemoRowFlexLineContainer.alignment}" coldistance="10" rowdistance="10" >
<t:image id="g_5" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo0.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_6" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo1.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_7" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo2.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_8" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo4.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_9" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo5.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_10" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo6.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_11" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo0.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_12" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo1.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_13" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo2.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_14" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo4.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
</t:rowflexlinecontainer>

Flexible columns

The items of the ROWFLEXCOLUMNCONTAINER are arranged in one or more columns - dependent from the current height of the component.

The control is the vertical counter part to the ROWFLEXLINECONTAINER, in which the items are arranged in a dynamic number of rows.

Please note: the control is available in the FX-Client only. In the Swing-client the control is the same as the control ROWFLEXLINECONTAINER.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>

<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_16" text="Resize the screen vertically - the images below will be re-arranged accordingly." />
</t:row>
<t:rowflexcolumncontainer id="g_4" coldistance="10" rowdistance="10" >
<t:image id="g_5" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo0.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_6" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo1.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_7" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo2.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_8" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo4.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_9" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo5.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />
<t:image id="g_10" height="100" image="/images/pictures/photo6.gif" keepratio="false" width="100" />

Adaptive matrix area with spanning

The component ROWSPANMATRIXAREA is a very useful component for structuring adaptive forms. It arranges the content items within a matrix, so that width and height of the corresponding item are consistently positioned both vertically and horizontally.

The width is divided into columns - the size an number of columns is driven by the attribute MATRIXWIDTH.

Each content item (in the example: the FOLDABLEPANE instances) is placed into this column definition so that the result is a matrix of components, each one occupying the number of columns it requires by its content.

A content item (in the example: the FOLDABLEPANE holding the grid) can explicitly request the spanning of columns by setting its attribute COLSPAN.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSpans}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_4" objectbinding="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSpans}" rowdistance="10" padding="0" >
<t:row id="g_86" coldistance="20" >
<t:textpane id="g_89" text="This demo requires some screen width! So either expand your full browser to maximum size or use the slider to zoom out the whole component..." width="100%" />
<t:labelcontainer id="g_91" text="Zoom of adaptive demo area" >
<t:slider id="g_92" flush="true" flushtimer="500" majortickspacing="25" maxvalue="100" minortickspacing="5" minvalue="50" value="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSpans.scaleInt}" width="250" />
</t:labelcontainer>
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_83" >
<t:splitpane id="g_9" border="#00000010" dividerlocation="50" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:splitpanesplit id="g_10" padding="20" >
<t:rowdistance id="g_84" height="100%" />
<t:row id="g_54" >
<t:textpane id="g_55" align="center" text="...please resize the right side by using the split pane&#39;s divider..." width="60" />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_60" height="100%" />
</t:splitpanesplit>

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSpans}")

public class DemoAdaptiveSpans
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    int m_scaleInt = 100;
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoAdaptiveSpans(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoadaptivespans.xml"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoAdaptiveSpans}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public int getScaleInt() { return m_scaleInt; }
    public void setScaleInt(int value) { m_scaleInt = value; }
    
    public double getScaleDouble() 
    {
        if (m_scaleInt == 100) 
            return 1d;
        else
            return (double)m_scaleInt/100d;
    }

    public void onScaleIntAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Matrix area

The ROWMATRIXAREA is an adaptive container, arranging its content components within one or several rows.

Each contained component is measured - the one with the highest minimum width defines the sizing of the matrix, so that each column of the matrix has the same width. All the matrix components that are part of the same row receive the same height.

This is the XML layout definition:

Adaptive areas

Resize the screen horizontally and observer how the three blocks are arranged accordingly.

The component ROWADAPTIVEAREA arranges its content in one or several lines depending from the screen size. To do so it defines so called size categories according to a width which is available for the component.

The content is defined inside ADAPTIVEAREAITEM components, which themselves define their horizontal size depending from the size categories. In addition the component indicate if a line break should occur for which size category.

The size and position of each ADAPTAREAITEM component is defined by the attributes:
(.) ADAPTIVEWIDTHS ("<cat>:<width>;<cat>:<width>;...")
(.) ADAPTIVEBREAKS ("<cat>:<break true/false>;<cat>:<break true/false>;...")

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>

Adaptive line

(FX only - this component is not supported in Swing yet.)

Resize the window horizontally - if the width is below a certain level then the controls in the lines are rearranged.

The component ROWADAPTIVELINE is a row that by default arranges its content into one line.

If the available horizontal width is below a certain level (defined by attribute BREADPIXELS) then the line is split into two lines. All the components left of the BREAKDINDEX (by default 1) are moved into the first line, the other ones are moved into the second line.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoRowAdaptiveLine}" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" >
<t:rowadaptiveline id="g_2" breakindex="1" breakpixels="400" >
<t:label id="g_3" text="First name" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_4" width="100%" />
</t:rowadaptiveline>
<t:rowadaptiveline id="g_5" breakindex="1" breakpixels="400" >
<t:label id="g_6" text="Last Name" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_7" width="100%" />
</t:rowadaptiveline>
<t:rowadaptiveline id="g_8" breakindex="1" breakpixels="400" >
<t:label id="g_9" text="Street" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_10" width="100%" />
<t:coldistance id="g_11" width="5" />
<t:field id="g_12" width="30" />
</t:rowadaptiveline>
<t:rowadaptiveline id="g_13" breakindex="1" breakpixels="400" >
<t:label id="g_14" text="Town" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_15" width="70" />
<t:coldistance id="g_16" width="5" />
<t:field id="g_17" width="100%" />
</t:rowadaptiveline>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

Adaptive split area

Resize this demo in vertical and/or horizontal direction and observe what happens.

The ADAPTIVESPLITAREA renders two content areas - one on the left, one on the right if used with horizontal orientation, and one on the top, one on the bottom if used with vertical orientation.

If the available space is sufficient then both areas are rendered in parallel. If the space is not sufficient, then the first are will be shrinked automatically and is only shown if the user explicitly opens it.

The width when the conversion from two visible areas to one visible area is executed is defined by the minimum size of the second area. If the minimum size of this area is reached then the area before is shrinked. You also may directly set this with by using attribute SPLITSIZE.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSplitArea}" rowdistance="20" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_3" text="Orientation" width="100" />
<t:radiobutton id="g_4" flush="true" group="ORIENTATION" refvalue="horizontal" text="Horizontal" value="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSplitArea.orientation}" />
<t:coldistance id="g_5" width="10" />
<t:radiobutton id="g_6" flush="true" group="ORIENTATION" refvalue="vertical" text="Vertical" value="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSplitArea.orientation}" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_7" >
<t:adaptivesplitarea id="g_8" closetrigger="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSplitArea.closeTrigger}" height="100%" orientation="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSplitArea.orientation}" splitsize="500" width="100%" >

</t:row>
</t:pane>
<t:pane id="g_16" padding="20" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" >
<t:row id="g_17" >

Adaptive tile cotainer

The ADAPTIVETILECONTAINER component allows to place content components ("tiles") which are arranged within a matrix. If the screen space is not sufficient then several pages are created internally. The user can navigate between the pages by dragging and dropping, or by using the corresponding navigation buttons.

Contained components are measured by their defined (minimum) height. You may not use percentage sizing within the contained components.

This is the XML layout definition:

Adaptive toolbar

Resize the screen horizontally - either the toolbar content is shown as one line of components - or the toolbar content is condensed into one icon and shown when the user presses this icon.

The adaptive toolbar is a container holding components - typically buttons, icons, search fields etc. If there is enough screen space then the content is rendered in one row, one after the other. If the screen space is not sufficient then only one icon is drawn. If the user presses the icon then a dialog shows up in which the controls are shown one below the other.

If opened as popup dialog, the componentes by default will show up with their original size. By setting attribute EXPANDCOMPONENTSINPOPUP to "true" the component's will be automatically rendered with a width of 100% so that they all have the same width.

The default styling of the toolbar (style variant "default") comes with some own rendering of padding and borders. For embedding the toolbar into other components (e.g. into the ROWHEADER) use style "ccembeddable" which comes without padding, border and background coloring.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.defaultscreens.Statusbar;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.events.BaseActionEventRearrange;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoAdaptiveToolbar}")

public class DemoAdaptiveToolbar
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    String m_alignment = "left";
    boolean m_expandComponentsInPopup = false;
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoAdaptiveToolbar(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoadaptivetoolbar.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoAdaptiveToolbar}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public String getAlignment() { return m_alignment; }
    public void setAlignment(String value) { this.m_alignment = value; }

    public void onAction1(ActionEvent event)
    {
        Statusbar.outputSuccess("Button1 was pressed.");
    }
    
    public void onAction2(ActionEvent event)
    {
        Statusbar.outputSuccess("Button2 was pressed.");
    }
    
    public void onAction3(ActionEvent event)
    {
        Statusbar.outputSuccess("Button3 was pressed.");
    }
    
    public void onRearrangeAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (event instanceof BaseActionEventRearrange)
        {
            BaseActionEventRearrange e = (BaseActionEventRearrange)event;
            Statusbar.outputSuccess("Content of toolbar was rearranged. Current mode is:" + e.getRearrangeMode());
        }
    }

    public boolean getExpandComponentsInPopup() { return m_expandComponentsInPopup; }
    public void setExpandComponentsInPopup(boolean value) { this.m_expandComponentsInPopup = value; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Adaptive side area with button

The page bean components CCAdaptiveSideContentArea and CCAdaptiveSideContentAreaButton are two content areas:

(.) The left side content area is either shown as own area or is shown when pressing a button, if the screen space is not sufficient
(.) The right main content area is always shown

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoPBCCCAdaptiveSide}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_2" objectbinding="#{d.DemoPBCCCAdaptiveSide}" >
<t:rowheader id="g_3" coldistance="5" >
<t:pagebeancomponent id="g_4" pagebeanbinding="#{d.DemoPBCCCAdaptiveSide.button}" shownullcontent="true" />
<t:button id="g_8" text="Some button" width="100+" />
<t:button id="g_10" text="Some button" width="100+" />
</t:rowheader>
<t:rowline id="g_5" />
<t:row id="g_23" >
<t:pagebeancomponent id="g_6" pagebeanbinding="#{d.DemoPBCCCAdaptiveSide.contentArea}" shownullcontent="true" />
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import org.eclnt.ccaddons.pbc.CCAdaptiveSideContentArea;
import org.eclnt.ccaddons.pbc.CCAdaptiveSideContentAreaButton;
import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.defaultscreens.ModelessPopup;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

import appstock.ArticleSearchUI;
import appstock.ArticleStockUI;
import appstock.EmptyContentUI;
import appstock.logic.Article;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoPBCCCAdaptiveSide}")

public class DemoPBCCCAdaptiveSide
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    CCAdaptiveSideContentAreaButton m_button;
    CCAdaptiveSideContentArea m_contentArea;
    
    ArticleSearchUI m_articleSearch;
    EmptyContentUI m_emptyContent;
    ArticleStockUI m_articleStock;

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoPBCCCAdaptiveSide(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
        init();
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demopbcccadaptiveside.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoPBCCCAdaptiveSide}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public CCAdaptiveSideContentAreaButton getButton() { return m_button; }
    public CCAdaptiveSideContentArea getContentArea() { return m_contentArea; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    private void init()
    {
        // whole area and button
        m_contentArea = new CCAdaptiveSideContentArea();
        m_contentArea.setSideBeanBorder("right:1;color:#00000010");
        m_button = m_contentArea.createOpenerButton();
        // content taken from appstock demo...
        m_articleSearch = new ArticleSearchUI();
        m_articleSearch.prepare(new ArticleSearchUI.IListener()
        {
            @Override
            public void reactOnArticleSelected(Article a)
            {
                m_articleStock = new ArticleStockUI();
                m_articleStock.prepare(a,null);
                showStockInContentArea(a);
                m_button.closeSideBeanPopup();
            }
            @Override
            public void reactOnArticleDetailsShown(Article a, ModelessPopup p)
            {
            }
        });
        m_articleSearch.setWithArticlePopup(false);
        m_articleStock = null;
        m_emptyContent = new EmptyContentUI();
        m_contentArea.prepare(m_articleSearch,m_emptyContent,"300",800,true,new CCAdaptiveSideContentArea.IListener()
        {
            @Override
            public void reactOnSideContentShown()
            {
            }
            @Override
            public void reactOnSideContentHidden()
            {
            }
        });
    }

    private void showStockInContentArea(Article a)
    {
        if (m_articleStock == null)
        {
            m_articleStock = new ArticleStockUI();
        }
        m_articleStock.prepare(a,null);
        m_contentArea.setContentBean(m_articleStock);
        m_contentArea.setShowSideBeanAtSide(false);
    }
    
}

Size transfer - "100% flexibility"

Use the SIZETRANSFER component in order to add any adaptive functions to your layout processing that you want to implement on your own.

The SIZETRANSFER component transfers the actual current width/height of a certain PAINE to the server side. The transfer is done either by pixel value (default) or by size categories.

In the example you see:

1. There are size categories both for transferring the width and the height. The height is not relevant for the adaptive functions in this example so there is only one general "ALL"-height transferred.

2. Changes of the size are transferred without any further activity required (FLUSH set to true)

3. Changed of the size are transferred without any latency (FLUSHTIMER set to 0)

On server side the sizing of the icons is "calculated" based on the width category that is sent from the client side.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSizeTransfer1}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_2" objectbinding="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSizeTransfer1}" >
<t:row id="g_3" >

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.managedbean.IDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.pagebean.PageBean;
import org.eclnt.util.valuemgmt.ValueManager;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoAdaptiveSizeTransfer1}")

public class DemoAdaptiveSizeTransfer1
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    public void onSizeAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        String[] widthHeight = ValueManager.decodeCSV(m_size);
        String width = widthHeight[0];
        if ("LARGE".equals(width)) m_iconWidthHeight = 64;
        else if ("MEDIUM".equals(width)) m_iconWidthHeight = 48;
        else if ("SMALL".equals(width)) m_iconWidthHeight = 32;
        else if ("VERYSMALL".equals(width)) m_iconWidthHeight = 16;
    }

    int m_iconWidthHeight = 64;
    public int getIconWidthHeight() { return m_iconWidthHeight; }
 
    String m_size = "LARGE";
    public String getSize() { return m_size; }
    public void setSize(String value) { this.m_size = value; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    /* Listener to the user of the page bean. */
    public interface IListener extends Serializable
    {
    }
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    private IListener m_listener;
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoAdaptiveSizeTransfer1(IDispatcher dispatcher)
    {
        super(dispatcher);
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoadaptivesizetransfer1.jsp"; }
    public DemoAdaptiveSizeTransfer1(IWorkpageDispatcher dispatcher)
    {
        super(dispatcher);
        // TODO Auto-generated constructor stub
    }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoAdaptiveSizeTransfer1}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    /* Initialization of the bean. Add any parameter that is required within your scenario. */
    public void prepare(IListener listener)
    {
        m_listener = listener;
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Adaptive grid layout

The ADAPTIVEGRIDLAYOUTPANE is a variant of the normal GRIDLAYOUTPANE - so you controls are arranged in columns.

The adaptive character comes with the attribute ADAPTIVECOLINDICES. Here you define the re-arrangements of columns dependent from different widths that are available to the control.

In the example the grid has 6 columns - due to the control definitions that are placed inside.

The definition "1000:4-2" means that the layout is updated if the available size is lower than 1000: now each line is "broken" into 4 columns for the first part and 2 columns for the second part.

You can now do multiple definitions, e.g. "300:1-1-1-1-1-1;600:2-2-2;1000:4-2". Please pay attention to define the proper order of definitions: the lowest width first, the highest width last.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" >
<t:beanprocessing id="g_1" beanbinding="#{d.DemoAdaptiveGridLayout}" />
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_4" objectbinding="#{d.DemoAdaptiveGridLayout}" rowdistance="20" >
<t:row id="g_7" >
<t:textpane id="g_8" text="Change the size of this demo - either by resizing the whole browser window and/or by moving the split divider of the workplace." width="100%" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_6" >
<t:adaptivegridlayoutpane id="g_2" adaptivecolindices="300:1-1-1-1-1-1;600:2-2-2;1000:4-2" coldistance="#{ccstylevalue[&#39;@defaultcoldistance@&#39;]}" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue[&#39;@defaultrowdistance@&#39;]}" width="100%" >
<t:gridlayoutrow id="g_38" >
<t:label id="g_5" text="Some label" />
<t:field id="g_10" width="100%;100" />
<t:label id="g_12" text="Another label with long text" />
<t:field id="g_13" width="100%;100" />
<t:label id="g_21" text="Another label with long text" />
<t:field id="g_22" width="100%;100" />
</t:gridlayoutrow>
<t:gridlayoutrow id="g_15" >
<t:label id="g_16" text="Short l." />
<t:field id="g_17" width="100%;100" />
<t:label id="g_18" text="Short" />
<t:field id="g_19" width="100%;100" />
<t:label id="g_23" text="Short" />
<t:field id="g_24" width="100%;100" />
</t:gridlayoutrow>
<t:gridlayoutrow id="g_26" >
<t:label id="g_27" text="Short l." />
<t:field id="g_28" width="100%;100" />
<t:label id="g_29" text="Short" />
<t:field id="g_30" colspan="3" width="100%;100" />
</t:gridlayoutrow>
<t:gridlayoutrow id="g_32" >
<t:label id="g_33" text="Short l." />
<t:field id="g_34" colspan="3" width="100%;100" />
<t:label id="g_35" text="Short" />
<t:field id="g_36" width="100%;100" />
</t:gridlayoutrow>
</t:adaptivegridlayoutpane>
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
</t:layoutdefinition>

Runtime update of size

Dynamic Pane Sizing

A component provides a set of attributes, e.g. a pane component provides a height attribute.

An attribute can either be defined in a fix way (height="100") or it can be bound to a property of a managed bean. This example demonstrates how the height of a pane is controlled by a server side property.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.demoDynamicPaneSizing}" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:pane id="g_3" animatechangeofsize="true" background="#{ccstylevalue[&#39;@backgroundColorGreen@&#39;]}" height="#{d.demoDynamicPaneSizing.height}" padding="10" width="100%" >
<t:row id="e_149" >
<t:label id="e_150" text="First Name 1" width="120" />
<t:field id="e_151" text="firstName1" width="200" />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_4" />
<t:row id="e_145" >
<t:label id="e_146" text="First Name 2" width="120" />
<t:field id="e_147" text="firstName1" width="200" />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_5" />
<t:row id="e_141" >
<t:label id="e_142" text="First Name 3" width="120" />
<t:field id="e_143" text="firstName1" width="200" />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_6" />
<t:row id="e_137" >
<t:label id="e_138" text="First Name 4" width="120" />
<t:field id="e_139" text="firstName1" width="200" />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_7" />
<t:row id="e_133" >
<t:label id="e_134" text="First Name 5" width="120" />
<t:field id="e_135" text="firstName1" width="200" />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_8" />
<t:row id="e_129" >
<t:label id="e_130" text="First Name 6" width="120" />
<t:field id="e_131" text="firstName1" width="200" />
</t:row>

</t:row>

<t:row id="g_14" >
<t:button id="e_127" actionListener="#{d.demoDynamicPaneSizing.onIncreaseHeight}" text="Increase Height" />
<t:button id="g_15" actionListener="#{d.demoDynamicPaneSizing.onDecreaseHeight}" text="Decrease Height" />
<t:coldistance id="e_126" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_16" actionListener="#{d.demoDynamicPaneSizing.onHideShow}" text="Hide / Show" />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_17" height="20" />
<t:row id="g_18" >
<t:label id="g_19" text="Current height value: " />

<t:field id="g_21" background="#F0F0F0" enabled="false" text="#{d.demoDynamicPaneSizing.height}" width="100" />
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

public class DemoDynamicPaneSizing extends PageBean
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    int m_height = 100;
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    public DemoDynamicPaneSizing(IWorkpageDispatcher dispatcher)
    {
        super(dispatcher);
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
        
    public int getHeight() { return m_height; }    
    
    public void onIncreaseHeight(ActionEvent ae)
    {
        m_height += 50;
    }
    
    public void onDecreaseHeight(ActionEvent ae)
    {
        m_height -= 50;
    }
    
    public void onHideShow(ActionEvent ae)
    {
        if (m_height != 0)
            m_height = 0;
        else
            m_height = 100;
    }
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    

}

Animated change of size

By setting attribute ANIMATECHANGEOFSIZE you can animate a change of the WIDTH and/or the HEIGHT of the component.

Please note: this attribute is only available within the FX client.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" objectbinding="#{d.DemoAnimateChangeOfSize}">
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_3" stylevariant="ccbig" text="Toggling between 2 pixel size definitions" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_4" >
<t:pane id="g_5" animatechangeofsize="true" background="#00000010" padding="10" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" width="#{d.DemoAnimateChangeOfSize.paneWidth}" >
<t:row id="g_6" >
<t:label id="g_7" text="Some label" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_8" text="Some field" width="100%" />
</t:row>

<t:row id="g_36" >
<t:label id="g_37" text="Some label" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_38" text="Some field" width="100%" />
</t:row>
