This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.defaultscreens.Statusbar;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.events.BaseActionEventSlideContainer;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.pagebean.PageBean;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoSlideContainer}")

public class DemoSlideContainer
    extends PageBean
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    public class ColorsItem extends Object implements java.io.Serializable
    {
        String m_color;
        public String getColor() { return m_color; }
        public void setColor(String value) { this.m_color = value; }

    }
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    String[] hexs = new String[] {"FF","C0","80","40","00"};
    List<ColorsItem> m_colors = new ArrayList<ColorsItem>();
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoSlideContainer(IWorkpageDispatcher dispatcher)
    {
        super(dispatcher);
        // create colors
        for (int ir=0; ir<hexs.length; ir++)
        {
            for (int ig=0; ig<hexs.length; ig++)
            {
                for (int ib=0; ib<hexs.length; ib++)
                {
                    ColorsItem c = new ColorsItem();
                    c.m_color = "#" + hexs[ir] + hexs[ig] + hexs[ib];
                    m_colors.add(c);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoslidecontainer.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoSlideContainer}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public List<ColorsItem> getColors() { return m_colors; }
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
}

Interactive time line

The SLIDECONTAINER sends an event to server side when being moved by the user. The event's data includes:

1. the current pixel position of the content inside the container.
2. the current pixel width of the container
3. the current pixel width of the content

In addition the current pixel-shift-value also is automatically transferred into its assigned property (here: "pixelShift"). This property serves both for passing the current shift from the client to the server and for passing some updated value from the server to the client. In the example the client's value is rounded on server side so that the shift is always starting at some quarter of an hour.

In the example this information is used for calculating the "time position" of the time line, that is rendered as content of the SLIDECONTAINER component.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTimeline}" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" >
<t:row id="g_19" >
<t:label id="g_20" stylevariant="ccbig" text="Some schedule" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_21" >
<t:slidecontainer id="g_22" actionListener="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTimeline.onSlideContainerAction}" border="0" orientation="horizontal" value="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTimeline.pixelShift}" width="100%" >
<t:pane id="g_23" >
<t:row id="g_24" >
<t:schedule id="g_25" height="40" numberofblocks="24" padding="0" schedulemax="24" width="4000" >
<t:repeat id="g_26" listbinding="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTimeline.scheduleHours}" >
<t:scheduleitem id="g_27" border="0" resizingenabled="false" scheduleleft=".{hour}" schedulewidth="1" >
<t:pane id="g_28" >
<t:row id="g_29" >
<t:coldistance id="g_30" width="3" />
<t:label id="g_31" align="left" text=".{hourString}" width="100%" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_32" >
<t:schedule id="g_33" background="#00000000" border="0" height="100%" numberofblocks="4" padding="0" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:scheduleitem>
</t:repeat>
</t:schedule>
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:slidecontainer>
</t:row>
<t:rowline id="g_34" />
<t:row id="g_35" >
<t:label id="g_36" text="Pixel shift" width="100" />
<t:formattedfield id="g_37" flush="true" flushtimer="1000" format="int" value="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTimeline.pixelShift}" width="100" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_38" >
<t:label id="g_39" text="This is as time" width="100" />
<t:formattedfield id="g_40" accessiblename="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTimeline.pixelShiftAsTime}" enabled="false" flush="true" flushtimer="1000" format="time" timezone="UTC" value="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTimeline.pixelShiftAsTime}" width="100" />
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.defaultscreens.Statusbar;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.events.BaseActionEventSlideContainer;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.pagebean.PageBean;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageContainer;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoSlideContainer}")

public class DemoSlideContainerTimeline
    extends PageBean
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    public class ScheduleHoursItem extends Object implements java.io.Serializable
    {
        int i_hour;
        String i_hourString;
        public ScheduleHoursItem(int hour)
        {
            i_hour = hour;
            i_hourString = "0" + i_hour+":00";
            if (i_hourString.length() > 5)
                i_hourString = i_hourString.substring(i_hourString.length()-5);
        }
        public int getHour()
        {
            return i_hour;
        }
        public String getHourString() 
        { 
            return i_hourString; 
        }
    }
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    int m_pixelShift = 0;
    long m_pixelShiftAsTime = 0;
    List<ScheduleHoursItem> m_scheduleHours = new ArrayList<ScheduleHoursItem>();
    int m_totalPixels = 0;
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoSlideContainerTimeline(IWorkpageDispatcher dispatcher)
    {
        super(dispatcher);
        // create schedule
        for (int i=0; i<24; i++)
        {
            ScheduleHoursItem shi = new ScheduleHoursItem(i);
            m_scheduleHours.add(shi);
        }
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoslidecontainer.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoSlideContainer}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public List<ScheduleHoursItem> getScheduleHours() { return m_scheduleHours; }
    
    public int getPixelShift() { return m_pixelShift; }
    public void setPixelShift(int value) { this.m_pixelShift = value; }

    public long getPixelShiftAsTime() { return m_pixelShiftAsTime; }
   
    public void onSlideContainerAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (event instanceof BaseActionEventSlideContainer)
        {
            BaseActionEventSlideContainer e = (BaseActionEventSlideContainer)event;
            Statusbar.outputSuccess("Slide was executed: " + e.getPixelShift() + "/" + e.getPixelWidth() + "/" + e.getContentPixelWidth());
            m_totalPixels = e.getContentPixelWidth();
            // round to quarters of an hour
            long pat = Math.round(((double)m_pixelShift / (double)m_totalPixels) * 3600000d * 24d);
            pat = Math.round((double)pat/900000) * 900000;
            m_pixelShiftAsTime = pat;
            m_pixelShift = (int)Math.round( (double)pat/(3600000d*24d) * (double)e.getContentPixelWidth());
        }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Triple content

Uuuh, this usage type of the SLIDECONTAINER is not really simple to understand... - but it provides some nice features!

By setting attribute TRIPLESIZECONTAINER to "true" some inner issues happen:

1. the content is automatically sized so that its width is three times the width of the container. As consequence you may always slide the content to both sides and you automatically have "enough content" to be shown to the user.

2. the meaning of PIXELSHIFT is shifted as well - assuming that "0" is exactly the position to show the middle part of the content.

As consequence you can easily define scenarios with "infinite content" to the left and right.

Please note: at server side your application must reset the pixel shift to "0" every time the content is recalculated so that the client switches back to show the middle part of the content.

(In the text above we assumed that the SLIDECONTAINER is used with ORIENTATION "horizontal". The triple-size-feature is available with vertical orientation as well, of course. In this case the height of the content is the one to be explicitly sized.)

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_4" objectbinding="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple}" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" >
<t:row id="g_12" >
<t:label id="g_13" stylevariant="ccbig" text="Some numbers..." />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_1" >
<t:slidecontainer id="g_7" actionListener="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple.onSlideAction}" triplesizecontent="true" value="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple.pixelShift}" width="100%" >
<t:pane id="g_10" >
<t:row id="g_11" >
<t:pane id="g_8" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_9" >
<t:repeat id="g_30" listbinding="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple.numbersLeft}" >
<t:pane id="g_31" bgpaint="bgbackground(#00000000,#00000020,horizontal)" height="50" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_14" >
<t:label id="g_15" align="center" cutwidth="true" text=".{value}" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:repeat>
</t:row>
</t:pane>
<t:pane id="g_17" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_18" >
<t:repeat id="g_19" listbinding="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple.numbers}" >
<t:pane id="g_20" bgpaint="bgbackground(#00000000,#00000020,horizontal)" height="50" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_21" >
<t:label id="g_22" align="center" cutwidth="true" text=".{value}" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:repeat>
</t:row>
</t:pane>

<t:row id="g_27" >

</t:row>

<t:formattedfield id="g_16" align="right" enabled="false" format="int" value="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple.startValue}" width="50" />
<t:coldistance id="g_39" width="5" />
<t:label id="g_36" text="to" />
<t:coldistance id="g_40" width="5" />
<t:formattedfield id="g_37" align="right" enabled="false" format="int" value="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple.endValue}" width="50" />

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.events.BaseActionEventSlideContainer;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDispatchedPageBean;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple}")

public class DemoSlideContainerTriple
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public class NumbersItem extends Object implements java.io.Serializable
    {
        int m_index;
        public int getValue() { return m_index+m_numberShift; }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    List<NumbersItem> m_numbers = new ArrayList<NumbersItem>();
    List<NumbersItem> m_numbersLeft = new ArrayList<NumbersItem>();
    List<NumbersItem> m_numbersRight = new ArrayList<NumbersItem>();
    int m_pixelShift = 0;
    int m_numberShift = 0;

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoSlideContainerTriple(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
        for (int i=0; i<10; i++)
        {
            {
                NumbersItem ni = new NumbersItem();
                ni.m_index = i-10;
                m_numbersLeft.add(ni);
            }
            {
                NumbersItem ni = new NumbersItem();
                ni.m_index = i;
                m_numbers.add(ni);
            }
            {
                NumbersItem ni = new NumbersItem();
                ni.m_index = i+10;
                m_numbersRight.add(ni);
            }
        }
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoslidecontainertriple.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoSlideContainerTriple}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public List<NumbersItem> getNumbers() { return m_numbers; }
    public List<NumbersItem> getNumbersLeft() { return m_numbersLeft; }
    public List<NumbersItem> getNumbersRight() { return m_numbersRight; }

    public int getPixelShift() { return m_pixelShift; }
    public void setPixelShift(int value) { this.m_pixelShift = value; }

    public int getStartValue() { return m_numberShift; }
    public int getEndValue() { return m_numberShift+10; }

    public void onSlideAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (event instanceof BaseActionEventSlideContainer)
        {
            BaseActionEventSlideContainer e = (BaseActionEventSlideContainer)event;
            m_numberShift = m_numberShift + (int)Math.round( (double)m_pixelShift/(double)e.getPixelWidth() * 10);
            m_pixelShift = 0; // reset is important!
        }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Synchronous sliding

In the demo the master container position is propagated to the slide containers below.

The coupling is done via the attributes MASTERID and MASTERIDTOFOLLOW: the MASTERID is defined with the leading slide container, the other ones reference the master by defining the same id in the attribute MASTERIDTOFOLLOW.

Only the master slide container is the active one - the other ones can not be slided on their owns anymore. And they will also not send or receive any data from the server side.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoSlideContainerMasterSlave}" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_3" stylevariant="ccbig" text="This is the master slide container:" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_4" >
<t:slidecontainer id="g_5" actionListener="#{d.DemoSlideContainerMasterSlave.onSliderAction}" height="100" masterid="MASTER" triplesizecontent="true" value="#{d.DemoSlideContainerMasterSlave.position}" width="100%" >
<t:pane id="g_6" >
<t:row id="g_7" >
<t:button id="g_8" height="100%" text="I take the lead!" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_9" height="100%" text="I take the lead!" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_10" height="100%" text="I take the lead!" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:slidecontainer>
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_11" >
<t:label id="g_12" text="Slide the content to the left and to the right." />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_13" height="5" />
<t:row id="g_14" >
<t:label id="g_15" text="Current position" width="100" />
<t:label id="g_16" text="#{d.DemoSlideContainerMasterSlave.position}" />
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_17" height="50" />
<t:row id="g_18" >
<t:label id="g_19" stylevariant="ccbig" text="...and these are threefollowing slide container:" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_20" >
<t:slidecontainer id="g_21" height="50" masteridtofollow="MASTER" triplesizecontent="true" width="100%" >
<t:pane id="g_22" >
<t:row id="g_23" >
<t:button id="g_24" height="100%" text="We" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_25" height="100%" text="We" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_26" height="100%" text="We" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:slidecontainer>
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_27" >
<t:slidecontainer id="g_28" height="50" masteridtofollow="MASTER" triplesizecontent="true" width="100%" >
<t:pane id="g_29" >
<t:row id="g_30" >
<t:button id="g_31" height="100%" text="will" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_32" height="100%" text="will" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_33" height="100%" text="will" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:slidecontainer>
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_34" >
<t:slidecontainer id="g_35" height="50" masteridtofollow="MASTER" triplesizecontent="true" width="100%" >
<t:pane id="g_36" >
<t:row id="g_37" >
<t:button id="g_38" height="100%" text="follow!" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_39" height="100%" text="follow!" width="100%" />
<t:button id="g_40" height="100%" text="follow!" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:slidecontainer>
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

Blockable Area

Basics

The BLOCKABLEAREA is a container component in which you can arrange exactly one other component as content.

When setting the attribute BLOCKED of the component to value "false" then the content of the BLOCKABLEAREA is completely blocked for user interaction. In addition some shading is arranged in front of the content so that the user receives some visual feed back.

BLOCKABLEAREA components can be nested.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoBlockableArea}" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_3" text="Outer block" width="100" />
<t:button id="g_4" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableArea.onBlockAction}" text="Block / unblock" />
<t:coldistance id="g_5" width="50" />
<t:checkbox id="g_6" flush="true" selected="#{d.DemoBlockableArea.blocked}" text="Blocked" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_7" >
<t:label id="g_8" text="Inner block" width="100" />
<t:button id="g_9" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableArea.onInnerBlockAction}" text="Block / unblock" />
<t:coldistance id="g_10" width="50" />
<t:checkbox id="g_11" flush="true" selected="#{d.DemoBlockableArea.blockedInner}" text="Blocked" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_12" >
<t:blockablearea id="g_13" blocked="#{d.DemoBlockableArea.blocked}" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:foldablepane id="g_14" enabled="false" height="100%" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" text="Outer block" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_15" >
<t:label id="g_16" text="Some label" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_17" text="Some field" width="200" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_18" >
<t:label id="g_19" text="Some label" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_20" text="Some field" width="200" />
</t:row>

<t:label id="g_22" text="Some label" width="100" />

</t:row>

</t:row>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.pagebean.PageBean;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoBlockableArea}")

public class DemoBlockableArea
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    boolean m_blocked = false;
    boolean m_blockedInner;
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoBlockableArea(IWorkpageDispatcher dispatcher)
    {
        super(dispatcher);
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoblockablearea.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoBlockableArea}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public boolean getBlocked() { return m_blocked; }
    public void setBlocked(boolean value) { this.m_blocked = value; }

    public boolean getBlockedInner() { return m_blockedInner; }
    public void setBlockedInner(boolean value) { this.m_blockedInner = value; }

    public void onBlockAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_blocked = !m_blocked;
    }
    
    public void onInnerBlockAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_blockedInner = !m_blockedInner;
    }

    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Use case: Grid with Detail Area

This example shows a typical usage scenario for the BLOCKABLEAREA: when the user selects an item in the grid then the item is opened for editing. While editing, the area around the grid is blocked so that the user first must finish editing the item.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid}" rowdistance="10" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_3" text="Double click an item of the grid for editing." />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_4" coldistance="20" >
<t:blockablearea id="g_5" blocked="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.boolGridBlocked}" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:pane id="g_6" height="100%" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_7" >
<t:fixgrid id="g_8" height="100%" objectbinding="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.grid}" sbvisibleamount="30" width="100%" >
<t:gridcol id="g_9" text="Number" width="80" >
<t:label id="g_10" text=".{article.number}" />
</t:gridcol>
<t:gridcol id="g_11" text="Text" width="100%;100" >
<t:label id="g_12" text=".{article.text}" />
</t:gridcol>
<t:gridcol id="g_13" text="UoM" width="50" >
<t:label id="g_14" text=".{article.baseUnitOfMeasure}" />
</t:gridcol>
</t:fixgrid>
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_15" >
<t:button id="g_16" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.onCreateNewArticle}" text="Create new article" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:blockablearea>
<t:pane id="g_17" rendered="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.boolDetailAvailable}" rowalignmenty="top" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_18" >
<t:label id="g_19" text="Number" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_20" requestfocus="creation" text="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.selectedArticle.number}" width="100%;100" />
</t:row>

<t:label id="g_22" text="Text" width="100" />
<t:textarea id="g_23" height="100" text="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.selectedArticle.text}" width="100%;100" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_24" >
<t:label id="g_25" text="Unit of Measure" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_26" text="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.selectedArticle.baseUnitOfMeasure}" width="100%;100" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_27" >
<t:coldistance id="g_28" width="100" />
<t:button id="g_29" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.onDetailOKAction}" text="OK" width="100" />
<t:coldistance id="g_30" width="10" />
<t:button id="g_31" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.onDetailCancelAction}" text="Cancel" width="100" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:row>

<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.impl.FIXGRIDItem;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.impl.FIXGRIDListBinding;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDispatchedPageBean;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid2}")

public class DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public class Article implements Cloneable
    {
        String i_number;
        String i_text;
        String i_baseUnitOfMeasure;
        public String getNumber() { return i_number; }
        public void setNumber(String number) { i_number = number; }
        public String getText() { return i_text; }
        public void setText(String text) { i_text = text; }
        public String getBaseUnitOfMeasure() { return i_baseUnitOfMeasure; }
        public void setBaseUnitOfMeasure(String baseUnitOfMeasure) { i_baseUnitOfMeasure = baseUnitOfMeasure; }
        @Override
        protected Object clone() throws CloneNotSupportedException { return super.clone(); }
    }
    
    public class GridItem extends FIXGRIDItem implements java.io.Serializable
    {
        Article i_article;
        public GridItem(Article article)
        {
            i_article = article;
        }
        public Article getArticle() { return i_article; }
        @Override
        public void onRowExecute()
        {
            try
            {
                m_selectedArticle = (Article)i_article.clone();
                m_selectedArticleIsNew = false;
            }
            catch (Throwable t)
            {
                throw new Error(t);
            }
        }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem> m_grid = new FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem>();
    Article m_selectedArticle;
    boolean m_selectedArticleIsNew;

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
        for (int i=0; i<50; i++)
        {
            Article a = new Article();
            a.setText("Article " + i);
            a.setNumber("53000"+i);
            a.setBaseUnitOfMeasure("kg");
            m_grid.getItems().add(new GridItem(a));
        }
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoblockableareawithgrid2.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid2}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem> getGrid() { return m_grid; }
    public Article getSelectedArticle() { return m_selectedArticle; }
    public boolean getBoolDetailAvailable() { return m_selectedArticle != null; }
    public boolean getBoolGridBlocked() { return getBoolDetailAvailable(); }

    public void onDetailCancelAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_selectedArticle = null;
    }

    public void onDetailOKAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (m_selectedArticleIsNew == false)
        {
            m_grid.getSelectedItem().i_article = m_selectedArticle;
        }
        else
        {   
            m_grid.getItems().add(0,new GridItem(m_selectedArticle));
        }
        m_selectedArticle = null;
    }

    public void onCreateNewArticle(ActionEvent event)
    {
        m_selectedArticle = new Article();
        m_selectedArticleIsNew = true;
    }
}

Use case: Grid with Detail "Popup"

This example shows a typical usage scenario for the BLOCKABLEAREA: when the user selects an item in the grid then the item is opened for editing. While editing, the area around the grid is blocked so that the user first must finish editing the item.

In this example the dialog is internally layered using the PAINTAREA component: in this component there is the base layer covering the whole area and there is the detail layer serving as "pseudo-popup-dialog". The detail layer has a higher z-index than the base layer, so it is displayed on top if rendered.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid2}" rowdistance="10" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_3" text="Double click an item of the grid for editing." />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_4" >
<t:paintarea id="g_5" height="100%;400" width="100%;500" >
<t:paintareaitem id="g_6" bounds="0;0;100%;100%;5" movetofrontonmouseover="false" >
<t:blockablearea id="g_7" blocked="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.boolGridBlocked}" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:pane id="g_8" height="100%" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_9" >
<t:fixgrid id="g_10" height="100%" objectbinding="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.grid}" sbvisibleamount="30" width="100%" >
<t:gridcol id="g_11" text="Number" width="80" >
<t:label id="g_12" text=".{article.number}" />
</t:gridcol>
<t:gridcol id="g_13" text="Text" width="100%;100" >
<t:label id="g_14" text=".{article.text}" />
</t:gridcol>
<t:gridcol id="g_15" text="UoM" width="50" >
<t:label id="g_16" text=".{article.baseUnitOfMeasure}" />
</t:gridcol>
</t:fixgrid>
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_17" >
<t:button id="g_18" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.onCreateNewArticle}" text="Create new article" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:blockablearea>
</t:paintareaitem>
<t:paintareaitem id="g_19" background="#FFFFFF" bounds="50%;50%;400;300;6" boundsanchor="centermiddle" movetofrontonmouseover="false" rendered="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.boolDetailAvailable}" >
<t:pane id="g_20" >
<t:rowtitlebar id="g_21" text="Article Detail" />
<t:row id="g_22" >
<t:pane id="g_23" border="#c0c0c0" height="100%" padding="10" rowalignmenty="top" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_24" >
<t:label id="g_25" text="Number" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_26" requestfocus="creation" text="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.selectedArticle.number}" width="100%;100" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_27" >
<t:label id="g_28" text="Text" width="100" />
<t:textarea id="g_29" height="100%;100" text="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.selectedArticle.text}" width="100%;100" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_30" >
<t:label id="g_31" text="Unit of Measure" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_32" text="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.selectedArticle.baseUnitOfMeasure}" width="100%;100" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_33" >
<t:coldistance id="g_34" width="100" />
<t:button id="g_35" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.onDetailOKAction}" text="OK" width="100" />
<t:coldistance id="g_36" width="10" />
<t:button id="g_37" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid.onDetailCancelAction}" text="Cancel" width="100" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:paintareaitem>
</t:paintarea>
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

    extends PageBean

{

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    {

        public void setBaseUnitOfMeasure(String baseUnitOfMeasure) { i_baseUnitOfMeasure = baseUnitOfMeasure; }

        protected Object clone() throws CloneNotSupportedException { return super.clone(); }
    }

        {
            i_article = article;
        }

        {

            {

                m_selectedArticleIsNew = false;
            }
            catch (Throwable t)

                throw new Error(t);
            }
        }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members

    boolean m_selectedArticleIsNew;

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoblockableareawithgrid.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoBlockableAreaWithGrid}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public FIXGRIDListBinding<GridItem> getGrid() { return m_grid; }
    public Article getSelectedArticle() { return m_selectedArticle; }
    public boolean getBoolDetailAvailable() { return m_selectedArticle != null; }
    public boolean getBoolGridBlocked() { return getBoolDetailAvailable(); }

    public void onDetailCancelAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        m_selectedArticle = null;
    }

    public void onDetailOKAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (m_selectedArticleIsNew == false)
        {
            m_grid.getSelectedItem().i_article = m_selectedArticle;
        }
        else
        {   
            m_grid.getItems().add(0,new GridItem(m_selectedArticle));
        }
        m_selectedArticle = null;
    }

    public void onCreateNewArticle(ActionEvent event)
    {
        m_selectedArticle = new Article();
        m_selectedArticleIsNew = true;
    }
}

"Semi-modal" popup dialogs

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:row id="g_1" >
<t:blockablearea id="g_2" blocked="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaModelessPopup.blocked}" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:scrollpane id="g_3" background="#ffffff" height="100%" padding="20" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_4" >
<t:button id="g_5" actionListener="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaModelessPopup.onOpenPopupAction}" text="Open &#34;semi-modal&#34; popup" />
</t:row>
</t:scrollpane>
</t:blockablearea>
</t:row>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.defaultscreens.ModelessPopup;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.pagebean.IPageBean;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDefaultLifecycleListener;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDispatchedPageBean;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoBlockableAreaModelessPopup}")

public class DemoBlockableAreaModelessPopup
    extends WorkpageDispatchedPageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // inner classes
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // members
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    IPageBean m_currentPopupPageBean;
    ModelessPopup m_currentPopup;
    int m_popupWidth = 800;
    int m_popupHeight = 600;
    int m_popupLeft = -1;
    int m_popupTop = -1;

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoBlockableAreaModelessPopup(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
        getWorkpage().addLifecycleListener(new WorkpageDefaultLifecycleListener()
        {
            @Override
            public void reactOnShownInContentArea()
            {
                showCurrentPopup();
            }
            @Override
            public void reactOnHiddenInContentArea()
            {
                hideCurrentPopup();
            }
            
            @Override
            public void closeForced()
            {
                closeCurrentPopup();
                super.closeForced();
            }
        });
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demoblockableareamodelesspopup.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoBlockableAreaModelessPopup}"; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // public usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------


    public boolean getBlocked() 
    { 
        if (m_currentPopupPageBean == null) 
            return false; 
        else
            return true;
    }

    public void onOpenPopupAction(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (m_currentPopup != null)
            return;
        if (m_currentPopupPageBean == null)
            m_currentPopupPageBean = new DemoHelloWorld(getOwningDispatcher());
        showCurrentPopup();
    }
    
    private void showCurrentPopup()
    {
        if (m_currentPopup == null)
        {
            m_currentPopup = openModelessPopup(m_currentPopupPageBean,"My popup",m_popupWidth,m_popupHeight,new ModelessPopup.IModelessPopupListener()
            {
                public void reactOnPopupClosedByUser()
                {
                    closeCurrentPopup();
                }
            });
            if (m_popupLeft >= 0) m_currentPopup.setLeft(m_popupLeft);
            if (m_popupTop >= 0) m_currentPopup.setTop(m_popupTop);
        }
    }
    
    private void closeCurrentPopup()
    {
        if (m_currentPopupPageBean != null)
        {
            closePopup(m_currentPopupPageBean);
            m_currentPopupPageBean = null;
            m_currentPopup = null;
        }
    }
    
    private void hideCurrentPopup()
    {
        if (m_currentPopupPageBean != null)
        {
            closePopup(m_currentPopupPageBean);
            m_popupWidth = m_currentPopup.getWidth();
            m_popupHeight = m_currentPopup.getHeight();
            m_popupLeft = m_currentPopup.getLeft();
            m_popupTop = m_currentPopup.getTop();
            m_currentPopup = null;
        }
    }
    
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // private usage
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
}

Rolling Container Area

Scroll the content area to the bottom - and observe what happens in the title area:

The title of the top-most area stays on top, so that the user always sees the content of the area within its context.

A ROLLINGCONTAINERAREA contains several ROWCONTAINER components. Each of the ROWCONTAINER components has the following attributes:

. TEXT - a title
. ICONSLEFT - a list of icons on the left of the title
. ICONSRIGHT - a list of icons on the right of the title

The list of icons is following the scheme "<id>:<image>;<id>:<image>;...".

A ROLLINGCONTAINER has an action listener through which the event is passed, if user presses one of the icons.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoRollingContainerArea}" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:rollingcontainerarea id="g_3" height="100%" width="100%" >
<t:rollingcontainer id="g_4" actionListener="#{d.DemoRollingContainerArea.onContainer1Action}" iconsleft="ID1:/images/iconssvg/toleft_light_24x24.svg" iconsright="ID2:/images/iconssvg/camera_light_24x24.svg;ID3:/images/iconssvg/teacher_light_24x24.svg" innerpadding="10" text="Some form" >
<t:row id="g_5" >
<t:pane id="g_6" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_7" >
<t:label id="g_8" text="First name" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_9" width="100%" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_10" >
<t:label id="g_11" text="Last name" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_12" width="100%" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_13" >
<t:label id="g_14" text="Street" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_15" width="100%" />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_16" >
<t:label id="g_17" text="Town" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_18" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:row>
</t:rollingcontainer>
<t:rollingcontainer id="g_19" actionListener="#{d.DemoRollingContainerArea.onContainer2Action}" iconsleft="ID1:/images/iconssvg/toleft_light_24x24.svg" innerpadding="0" text="Some map" >
<t:row id="g_20" >
<t:pane id="g_21" height="500" width="100%" >
<t:row id="g_22" >
<t:osmviewer id="g_23" height="100%" latitude="8" longitude="7" osmzoom="10" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:pane>
</t:row>
</t:rollingcontainer>
<t:rollingcontainer id="g_24" innerpadding="0" text="Some container" >
<t:row id="g_25" >
<t:tabbedpane id="g_26" height="200" width="100%" >
<t:tabbedpanetab id="g_27" text="First" />
<t:tabbedpanetab id="g_28" text="Second" />
</t:tabbedpane>
</t:row>
</t:rollingcontainer>
<t:rollingcontainer id="g_29" innerbackground="#E0FFE0" text="Some image" >
<t:row id="g_30" >
<t:coldistance id="g_31" width="100%" />
<t:image id="g_32" height="200" image="/images/pictures/adressbuch.png" width="300" />
<t:coldistance id="g_33" width="100%" />
</t:row>
</t:rollingcontainer>
</t:rollingcontainerarea>
</t:row>
</t:rowdemobodypane>
<t:pageaddons id="g_pa"/>
</t:layoutdefinition>

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;
import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.defaultscreens.Statusbar;
import org.eclnt.jsfserver.elements.events.BaseActionEventRollingContainerIconInvoke;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;
import org.eclnt.workplace.WorkpageDispatchedPageBean;

import javax.faces.event.ActionEvent;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoRollingContainerArea}")

public class DemoRollingContainerArea
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    public DemoRollingContainerArea(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);        
    }

    public String getPageName() { return "/workplace/demorollingcontainerarea.jsp"; }
    public String getRootExpressionUsedInPage() { return "#{d.DemoRollingContainerArea}"; }

    public void onContainer1Action(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (event instanceof BaseActionEventRollingContainerIconInvoke)
        {
            BaseActionEventRollingContainerIconInvoke e = (BaseActionEventRollingContainerIconInvoke)event;
            Statusbar.outputSuccessWithPopup("Icon was pressed in Container 1, id = " + e.getIconId() +".");
        }
    }

    public void onContainer2Action(javax.faces.event.ActionEvent event) 
    {
        if (event instanceof BaseActionEventRollingContainerIconInvoke)
        {
            BaseActionEventRollingContainerIconInvoke e = (BaseActionEventRollingContainerIconInvoke)event;
            Statusbar.outputSuccessWithPopup("Icon was pressed in Container 2, id = " + e.getIconId() +".");
        }
    }
}

Pane with synchronized Columns

When using the default CaptainCasa containers, then each row inside the container is rendered individually. The controls within the row are NOT synchronized.

The COLSYNCHEDPANE container behaves in a different way: the width of the columns are synchronized across its contained rows. (This is very close to the behavior of nomal HTML tables...) This makes the arranging of controls simpler in certain scenarios.

This is the XML layout definition:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<t:layoutdefinition xmlns:t="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/t" xmlns:tpbc="http://www.CaptainCasa.com/controllibrary/tpbc" >
<t:rowdemobodypane id="g_1" objectbinding="#{d.DemoColSynchedPane}" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" >
<t:row id="g_2" >
<t:label id="g_3" font="size:14" text="Synchronized Columns..." />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_4" >
<t:colsynchedpane id="g_5" border="#00000030" coldistance="5" padding="10" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" >
<t:colsynchedrow id="g_6" >
<t:label id="g_7" text="First Name" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_8" width="100" />
<t:button id="g_9" text="Clear" />
</t:colsynchedrow>
<t:colsynchedrow id="g_10" >
<t:label id="g_11" text="Last Name" width="100" />
<t:field id="g_12" width="100" />
<t:button id="g_13" text="Clear" />
</t:colsynchedrow>
<t:colsynchedrowdistance id="g_14" height="20" />
<t:colsynchedrow id="g_15" >
<t:label id="g_16" text="Marital Status" width="100" />
<t:checkbox id="g_17" text="Married" />
<t:button id="g_18" text="Clear" />
</t:colsynchedrow>
</t:colsynchedpane>
</t:row>
<t:rowdistance id="g_19" height="10" />
<t:row id="g_20" >
<t:label id="g_21" font="size:14" text="With percentage Sizing..." />
</t:row>
<t:row id="g_22" >
<t:colsynchedpane id="g_23" border="#00000030" coldistance="5" padding="10" rowdistance="#{ccstylevalue['@defaultrowdistance@']}" width="100%" >

This is the Java code:

package workplace;

import java.io.Serializable;

import org.eclnt.editor.annotations.CCGenClass;
import org.eclnt.workplace.IWorkpageDispatcher;

@CCGenClass (expressionBase="#{d.DemoColSynchedPane}")

public class DemoColSynchedPane
    extends PageBean 
    implements Serializable
{
    int m_fieldwidth = 100;
    public int getFieldwidth() { return m_fieldwidth; }
    public void setFieldwidth(int value) { this.m_fieldwidth = value; }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // constructors & initialization
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------

    public DemoColSynchedPane(IWorkpageDispatcher workpageDispatcher)
    {
        super(workpageDispatcher);       
        this.initRefComponent("colsynchedpane");
    }

}
